<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1318_cdabce-f3 kvs-lg-false kvs-md-false"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1318_6a4278-bc wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-1-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_6a4278-bc"><em>Let&#8217;s check off our travel bucket list!</em></h2>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id1318_b8ad3a-2f alignfull kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-layout-bottom-sep kt-row-sep-type-crv"><svg viewBox="0 0 1000 100" preserveAspectRatio="none"><path d="M1000,100c0,0 -270.987,-98 -500,-98c-229.013,0 -500,98 -500,98l1000,0Z" /></svg></div><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-left-golden kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1318_f16108-9b"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading1318_f83d33-28 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_f83d33-28">Welcome To Destination Check-off!</h1>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p class="kt-adv-heading1318_a9c861-03 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_a9c861-03"><strong>Real trips. Real planning. Real itineraries.</strong></p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading1318_11a1d7-e3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_11a1d7-e3">Hi, I’m Anu, a full-time professional who knows just how precious vacation days are and how important it is to make every trip count. I love the planning phase almost as much as the trip itself, doing in-depth research to make the most of the time and money invested in visiting each destination.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading1318_c182da-9a wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_c182da-9a">I’m a California local and a lifelong travel enthusiast. Over the past 20 years, I’ve explored destinations across the United States, Canada, Mexico, Europe, and Asia, from quick getaways to longer bucket list trips.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading1318_b4152d-b7 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_b4152d-b7">On Destination Checkoff, you’ll find itineraries and destination guides based entirely on places I’ve personally experienced. Every guide is shaped by firsthand travel, real planning, and practical tips to help you travel with confidence and start checking off your travel bucket list.</p>
</div></div>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1318_c1a858-0d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_c1a858-0d">Where To Next?</h2>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1318_5d81cd-72"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1318_182219-48 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_182219-48">Hawaii</h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p class="kt-adv-heading1318_025638-63 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1318_025638-63">Hawaii is one of my favorite vacation destinations. I’ve spent at least a week on the Big Island, Maui, and Oahu, exploring each island in depth. My Hawaii itineraries and guides are built from detailed, firsthand experiences to help you plan with confidence.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns1318_cbd2a7-ab"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn1318_9927e5-64 kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-fixed kb-btn-global-fill kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://destinationcheckoff.com/hawaii/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Explore Hawaii!</span></a></div>
</div></div>
